Step 1: Coarse pass to find approximate locations\n    t_coarse = np.linspace(-search_range, search_range, coarse_samples)\n    dt_coarse = t_coarse[1] - t_coarse[0]\n    f_coarse = np.array([forward(e_j * t) for t in t_coarse])\n    \n    # Forward slopes\n    forward_slopes = (f_coarse[1:] - f_coarse[:-1]) / dt_coarse\n    changes = np.diff(forward_slopes)\n    abs_changes = np.abs(changes)\n    \n    threshold = 1e-5\n    significant = np.where(abs_changes > threshold)[0]\n    \n    candidates_approx = []\n    i = 0\n    while i < len(significant):\n        idx = significant[i]\n        if idx + 1 < len(changes) and abs_changes[idx+1] > threshold and np.sign(changes[idx]) == np.sign(changes[idx+1]):\n            c0 = changes[idx]\n            c1 = changes[idx+1]\n            total_change = c0 + c1\n            if abs(total_change) > 1e-10:\n                t_approx = t_coarse[idx+1] + dt_coarse * c0 / total_change\n                candidates_approx.append(t_approx)\n                i += 2\n                continue\n        i += 1\n    \n    # Step 2: For each candidate, refine with finer grid in a narrow window\n    refined_breakpoints = []\n    for t_approx in candidates_approx:\n        # Search in [t_approx - 2*dt_coarse, t_approx + 2*dt_coarse]\n        window = 2 * dt_coarse\n        t_fine = np.linspace(t_approx - window, t_approx + window, fine_samples)\n        dt_fine = t_fine[1] - t_fine[0]\n        f_fine = np.array([forward(e_j * t) for t in t_fine])\n        \n        forward_slopes_fine = (f_fine[1:] - f_fine[:-1]) / dt_fine\n        changes_fine = np.diff(forward_slopes_fine)\n        abs_changes_fine = np.abs(changes_fine)\n        \n        significant_fine = np.where(abs_changes_fine > threshold)[0]\n        \n        found = False\n        i = 0\n        while i < len(significant_fine):\n            idx = significant_fine[i]\n            if idx + 1 < len(changes_fine) and abs_changes_fine[idx+1] > threshold and np.sign(changes_fine[idx]) == np.sign(changes_fine[idx+1]):\n                c0 = changes_fine[idx]\n                c1 = changes_fine[idx+1]\n                total_change = c0 + c1\n                if abs(total_change) > 1e-10:\n                    t_refined = t_fine[idx+1] + dt_fine * c0 / total_change\n                    refined_breakpoints.append((t_refined, total_change))\n                    found = True\n                    i += 2\n                    continue\n            i += 1\n        \n        if not found:\n            # Build adjacency based on close |t*Δ| values and different directions\n    adj = np.zeros((n, n), dtype=bool)\n    \n    for i in range(n):\n        for j in range(i+1, n):\n            di = int(sorted_bps[i, 0])\n            dj = int(sorted_bps[j, 0])\n            if di == dj:\n                continue\n            \n            inv_i = sorted_bps[i, 3]\n            inv_j = sorted_bps[j, 3]\n            abs_max = max(inv_i, inv_j)\n            if abs_max > 1e-6:\n                rel_diff = abs(inv_i - inv_j) / abs_max\n                if rel_diff < 0.02:  # Within 2%\n                    adj[i, j] = adj[j, i] = True\n    \n    # Find connected components\n    used = set()\n    clusters = []\n    \n    for i in range(n):\n        if i in used:\n            continue\n        cluster = [i]\n        used.add(i)\n        \n        changed = True\n        while changed:\n            changed = False\n            for j in range(n):\n                if j not in used:\n                    for k in cluster:\n                        if adj[j, k]:\n                            cluster.append(j)\n                            used.add(j)\n                            changed = True\n                            break\n        clusters.append(cluster)\n    \n    print(f\"\\nRaw clusters: {len(clusters)}\")\n    for k, cluster in enumerate(clusters):\n        dirs = [int(sorted_bps[i, 0]) for i in cluster]\n        print(f\"  Cluster {k}: size={len(cluster)}, dirs={sorted(set(dirs))}\")\n    \n    # Filter clusters with at least 2 unique directions\n    clusters = [c for c in clusters if len(set(int(sorted_bps[i, 0]) for i in c)) >= 2]\n    \n    print(f\"\\nAfter filtering: {len(clusters)} clusters\")\n    \n    # Build recovered A1\n    A1_recovered = np.zeros((len(clusters), 10))\n    \n    for k, cluster in enumerate(clusters):\n        print(f\"\\nCluster {k} (size {len(cluster)}):\")\n        row = np.zeros(10)\n        for i in cluster:\n            bp = sorted_bps[i]\n            j = int(bp[0])\n            val = bp[4]\n            if row[j] == 0:\n                row[j] = val\n            else:\n                row[j] = (row[j] + val) / 2\n            print(f\"  dir={j}, t={bp[1]:+.10f}, -1/t={val:+.8f}\")\n        \n        norm = np.linalg.norm(row)\n        if norm > 0:\n            row = row / norm\n        A1_recovered[k, :] = row\n    \n    return A1_recovered\n\n\nif __name__ == '__main__':\n    A1_stolen = recover_A1()\n    if A1_stolen is not None and A1_stolen.shape[0] > 0:\n        np.save('/app/stolen_A1.npy', A1_stolen)\n        print(f\"\\nSaved stolen A1 to /app/stolen_A1.npy\")\n        print(f\"Shape: {A1_stolen.shape}\")\n        print(\"Stolen A1 (rows normalized):\")\n        np.set_printoptions(precision=6, suppress=True, linewidth=200)\n        print(A1_stolen)\n        print(\"\\nDone!\")\n    else:\n        print(\"Failed to recover A1\")\nENDOFFILE\n",
